### Q10: Le Départ Mesuré (The Departure Calibration)

**Scenario:** At the conclusion of a four-hour evening at a private residence in Uccle hosted by a peer-Grande-Dame and her senior Patriarche husband, the senior Grande-Dame of sixty-four sits with her senior Patriarche husband as the post-coffee moment settles; several guests have begun to rise. In the senior-couple departure tradition the Grande-Dame is the natural rhythm-anchor — the senior-female signal triggers the spousal-coordinated rise. The next ten minutes calibrate whether the Grande-Dame has internalised the senior-female generational departure-architecture as Grande-Dame-led spousal coordination — the discipline of timing the rhythm-anchor signal to honour the close without imposing senior-rhythm on the broader cohort's natural rhythm.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Time the rhythm-anchor signal at the natural fifth or sixth turn — late enough that the senior generation has not pre-empted the cohort's rhythm, early enough that the household's architectural close is honoured within the calibrated rhythm. The Grande-Dame signals the calibrated rise to her senior Patriarche husband through the brief composed glance of long-coordinated practice; the spousal-coordinated rise occurs within seconds. The Grande-Dame leads the approach to the host couple at the salon doorway with the composed warm farewell — the calibrated brief composed double-cheek-kiss appropriate to long-established peer-Grande-Dame acquaintance, the substantive farewell-remark naming a specific moment of the evening that signals senior-female generational-receipt of the architecture; the senior Patriarche husband's parallel farewell follows in the same register at the same calibrated brevity. Composed brief farewells to the immediate neighbours of the cluster, coordinated across the senior-couple pair. The coats are collected at the entrance and donned at the entrance; the household-departure operates as composed Grande-Dame-led senior-pair bearing through the threshold.

*The discipline is "Le Départ Mesuré" — the principle that the Belgian dinner-departure operates within a calibrated rhythm that honours the hostess; for the senior Grande-Dame the discipline carries the doubled weight that the senior generation often serves as the natural departure-rhythm-anchor for the broader cohort, and the senior-female rhythm-anchor signal must honour both the household's close-architecture and the broader cohort's natural-rhythm without imposing senior-rhythm on either. The fifth-or-sixth-turn timing signals composed senior-female architectural-reading; the Grande-Dame-led spousal-coordinated rise signals composed long-practiced household-bearing.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same Grande-Dame-led coordinated senior departure with brief private exchanges at the entrance — the Grande-Dame's brief private farewell with the peer-Grande-Dame on a foundation-matter, the senior Patriarche husband's brief parallel exchange with the host on a professional-matter — when the established peer-relationships warrant brief separate moments that do not prolong the broader coordinated departure-rhythm.

*The contemporary refinement permitting brief separate spousal moments at the entrance; the separate exchanges are composed and brief, calibrated to the relationship-architecture, never elaborated into prolonged independent senior departures.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Time the rhythm-anchor signal too early in senior-female-rhythm imposition that forces the broader cohort to depart before natural rhythm; time the signal too late in senior-extension that imposes on the host couple's natural close; allow the Grande-Dame-led coordination to drift into husband-led independent departure where the senior Patriarche initiates the rise; offer effusive matriarchal-affinity farewell beyond senior register's composed brief calibration; reappear in the salon after initial farewells; don the coat in the salon rather than at the entrance; or offer extended matriarchal-mentorship acknowledgement at the threshold to the peer-Grande-Dame that imposes Doyenne-narrative on the household close.

*All seven fail. The early senior-female-rhythm is "Doyenne-Lead Slip" — the imposition of senior-female rhythm on the broader cohort that the host couple registers as compositional gap. The late senior-extension is "Doyenne Doorway-Anchor" — the extension beyond the calibrated close that imposes on the household. The husband-led drift is "Asynchronous-Departure Doyenne" — the visible fragmentation of established Grande-Dame-led senior-couple bearing. The effusive matriarchal-affinity is "Generic-Effusion Doyenne" — the conversion of composed appreciation into performative senior-female-affinity inappropriate to senior register. The reappearance is "Doyenne Re-Entry" — the breach of the architectural close. The salon-coat is "Doyenne Salon-Coat" — the outerwear donned in the wrong room. The matriarchal-mentorship acknowledgement is "Staff-Direction Doyenne" — the senior-female narrative at the threshold that imposes Doyenne-register on the household close.*

**Historical Context:** Le Départ Mesuré for the senior Grande-Dame is preserved at the older Brussels patrician townhouse senior evenings — Uccle, Tervuren, Stockel, Boitsfort, Watermael — and at the country residences of Brabant Wallon at Lasne and La Hulpe, where the senior-female Grande-Dame-led coordinated household-bearing has been continuous practice across post-war generations. The convention persists in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp senior departure-traditions: at the Antwerp foundation senior evenings the Grande-Dame-led coordinated departure carries marginally more direct register in keeping with Antwerp commercial confidence, while at the Liège Cercle senior bourgeois evenings the departure runs marginally warmer in keeping with the Walloon convivial register.

Belgium — Phase 1 — Pillar 3: The Table — Level 2: The Practitioner — Cross-Demographic: Cavalier ↔ Demoiselle (M19-30 with V19-30 in Senior-Observed Rooms)

*Focus: The applied semi-public architecture calibrated to the lateral peer-engagement of the young Cavalier and the young Demoiselle within senior-rich Belgian elite rooms — the cluster-entry where the peers encounter one another under senior gaze (L'Abordage), the receiving-line cross-recognition in front of the senior Châtelaines (Calibration des Hôtes), the cross-regional Antwerp commercial-elite working-lunch with seniors observing the lateral peer-bearing (Le Déjeuner Professionnel), the calibrated lateral peer-bearing in the senior-observed cluster (La Calibration Latérale), the introduction-protocol when one peer introduces the other to a senior figure (Le Protocole de Présentation), the withheld lateral peer-formation at Brabant Wallon residence cellar tastings (La Discipline de Dégustation). The codes elevate beyond the foundational L1 register into the higher-stakes practice of senior-observed peer-engagement at Cercle Munster multi-table evenings, foundation-galas at Spa and Brabant Wallon, the Antwerp commercial-elite working lunches, and the multi-day Belgian elite calendar where the young Cavalier and young Demoiselle navigate peer-bearing in rooms of mature senior gaze. The senior Châtelaines and the senior Patriarche register read the calibrated lateral bearing as the marker of formation that has internalised the discipline of peer-engagement absorbing gender into substantive frame — neither flirt-drift nor over-formal drift surfaces, neither familiarity-cascade nor diffident-distance — the composed lateral peer-bearing that the senior cohort recognises as twin formations operating in calibrated parallel.*

### Q1: L'Abordage (The Reception Approach)

**Scenario:** At a small diplomatic reception held at one of the Etterbeek embassies, the young Cavalier of twenty-eight arrives mid-evening and recognises the young Demoiselle of twenty-six in a cluster of three near the salon's piano — the Demoiselle is in conversation with two senior figures, one of whom is the senior cultural attaché. The Cavalier and the Demoiselle have established professional acquaintance through a foundation-overlap; they have met perhaps four times across the prior eighteen months at comparable events. The cluster's primary speaker is the senior cultural attaché; the senior Châtelaine wife of the senior diplomat is at an adjacent cluster within sightline. The next thirty seconds calibrate whether the Cavalier's L'Abordage-bearing and the Demoiselle's acknowledgement-register operate within the lateral peer-discipline that the senior gaze reads precisely.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Cavalier approaches the cluster on the calibrated diagonal that the L'Abordage discipline preserves; the body angled three-quarters toward the cluster, the flute held at the lower-chest register. The Demoiselle's recognition of the approach must avoid both the brightening-warmth that would surface as flirt-drift register the senior Châtelaine wife at the adjacent cluster would read precisely, and the over-composed neutrality that would signal denial of the existing professional acquaintance. She calibrates her acknowledgement to the composed brief register she would offer any peer arriving at the cluster: composed neutral brief inclination, brief substantive recognition of the foundation-overlap context if the senior cultural attaché's running thread permits it. The Cavalier upon admission contributes to the cluster's running thread rather than to the recognition of the Demoiselle through cluster-frame conversion. The lateral peer-bearing operates: composed mutual recognition absorbed into the cluster-architecture, the senior gaze read precisely by both parties as the calibrating frame.

*The discipline is the joint calibration of the lateral peer-bearing under senior observation — for the Cavalier the cluster-entry must not surface the existing acquaintance through approach-rhythm or eye-contact pattern that would signal the Demoiselle as the cluster's substantive anchor; for the Demoiselle the recognition must not surface as either personal-warmth that would convert the cluster into mixed-register exchange or as over-correcting neutrality that would itself signal awareness of the senior gaze. The composed mutual brief acknowledgement absorbed into the cluster-architecture is the formed lateral peer-discipline; the senior Châtelaine wife at the adjacent cluster reads the calibrated absorption as the diagnostic moment confirming twin formations operating in calibrated parallel.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same lateral calibration with a brief substantive contribution from the Cavalier that explicitly addresses the senior cultural attaché rather than the Demoiselle — extending the running thread on the cultural-acquisition question — appropriate when the substantive standing has been recognised in prior foundation-evenings.

*The contemporary refinement when substantive contribution is welcomed; the Cavalier's contribution honours the senior cultural attaché's authority over the cluster and explicitly does not address the Demoiselle as primary interlocutor.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Approach the cluster with eye-contact pattern that locks onto the Demoiselle and signals her as the approach-anchor; allow the Demoiselle's brief acknowledgement to brighten into warmth that surfaces personal-register; pre-empt the running thread to bridge with the Demoiselle through reference to their prior foundation-overlap; the Demoiselle responds with smile-extension that matches the warmth-register and that the senior Châtelaine reads as flirt-drift; or both parties retreat into over-formal stiffness that signals their awareness of the senior gaze and registers as compositional gap of formed lateral peer-discipline.

*All five fail. The eye-contact lock is "Flirt-Drift Approach" — the conversion of cluster-architecture into Demoiselle-anchor that the senior Châtelaine wife reads precisely as compositional gap. The brightening warmth is "Personal-Register Surfacing" — the visible surfacing of acquaintance into warmth-register inappropriate to the senior-observed cluster. The bridge pre-emption is "Lateral Edge-Hold" — the conversion of cluster-thread into Cavalier-Demoiselle bridge that displaces the senior cultural attaché's authority over the running line. The smile-extension match is "Senior-Observed Posture-Slip" — the bilateral surfacing that the senior gaze reads as twin compositional gaps. The over-formal stiffness is "Over-Formal Cluster-Approach" — the awareness-of-senior-gaze that itself signals lateral peer-discipline uninternalised.*

**Historical Context:** L'Abordage for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Brussels diplomatic Etterbeek and Square Marie-Louise embassy receptions, where the senior diplomatic Châtelaines have continuously calibrated the lateral peer-bearing of younger generations across post-war diplomatic generations. The convention runs in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp foundation-circles: at the Antwerp commercial-elite receptions the lateral peer-bearing operates with marginally more direct register, while at the Liège Cercle bourgeois receptions the lateral register carries additional convivial warmth without surrendering the calibrated peer-discipline.

### Q2: Calibration des Hôtes (Multi-Host Calibration)

**Scenario:** Arriving at a foundation co-hosting evening at a private residence in Boitsfort, the young Cavalier of twenty-seven encounters the young Demoiselle of twenty-five at the receiving-line — she is one position ahead of him in the line, having just completed her greeting to the lady of the house and now turning to greet the co-hostess. The Cavalier knows the Demoiselle from prior foundation-evenings; the senior Châtelaines are watching the line continue. The next thirty seconds calibrate whether the lateral peer-encounter at the receiving-line preserves the architectural sequence rather than fracturing it through cross-greeting that would interrupt the Châtelaines' receiving rhythm.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Cavalier completes his greeting to the lady of the house with calibrated junior register; he then turns to the co-hostess as the Demoiselle is completing her greeting to the same co-hostess. The lateral encounter is calibrated to the receiving-line architecture: a brief composed nod from the Cavalier as the Demoiselle steps away from the co-hostess, a brief composed return-nod from the Demoiselle as she moves into the entrance hall. No verbal cross-exchange at the receiving-line; no extended eye-contact that would cause either Châtelaine to register the lateral peer-acquaintance as architectural disruption; no smile-warmth that would signal personal-register inappropriate to the receiving-line frame. The cross-acknowledgement absorbs into the line's architecture; the lateral peer-encounter is preserved as composed brief micro-moment between two structural sequences.

*The discipline is the joint preservation of the receiving-line architecture under lateral peer-encounter — both parties register the cross-encounter without displacing the Châtelaines' receiving rhythm. For the Cavalier the brief nod must not extend into personal-register; for the Demoiselle the return-nod must not surface warmth that the lady of the house would read precisely from her receiving position. The composed mutual brief acknowledgement absorbed into the line's architecture is the formed lateral peer-discipline; the senior Châtelaines' receiving rhythm is preserved through the calibrated brevity.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same lateral calibration with a single composed verbal acknowledgement when the line behind both has paused — "ah, Margaux" or "Pierre" delivered at quiet volume in passing — appropriate when the line architecture has briefly opened and the verbal acknowledgement is brief enough to absorb without displacing the receiving rhythm.

*The contemporary refinement when the line architecture has briefly opened; the verbal acknowledgement is composed and brief, never elaborated into entrance-hall conversation.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Pause at the receiving-line to exchange brief words with the Demoiselle while the line behind continues; allow the cross-greeting to extend into smile-warmth that the receiving Châtelaines register as flirt-drift; cross the receiving-line architecture by stepping briefly toward the Demoiselle's position; offer extended verbal acknowledgement that displaces the Châtelaines' receiving rhythm; or pretend not to see the Demoiselle in over-formal denial that the Châtelaines themselves read as lateral peer-discipline uninternalised.

*All five fail. The line-pause exchange is "Flutter-Cross Acceptance" — the breach of receiving-line architecture through lateral peer-conversation that the receiving Châtelaines and the line behind register as compositional gap. The smile-warmth extension is "Cross-Greeting Drift" — the visible surfacing of personal-register at the receiving-line. The line-crossing step is "Familiarity Surface-Cross" — the architectural breach through movement against the line's flow. The extended verbal acknowledgement is "Senior-Châtelaine Reading-Slip" — the misreading of the Châtelaines' receiving rhythm as background to the lateral peer-encounter. The over-formal denial is "Over-Formal Acknowledgement" — the visible non-recognition that itself signals awareness of the lateral peer-acquaintance and registers as compositional gap.*

**Historical Context:** The multi-host architecture under lateral peer-encounter is preserved at the Brussels patrician townhouse foundation-evenings of Boitsfort, Watermael, Stockel, and Uccle, where the senior Châtelaines have continuously calibrated the lateral peer-bearing of younger generations during the receiving-line rhythm. The convention extends into the Flemish register with calibrated rhythms: at the Antwerp commercial-elite foundation evenings the lateral receiving-line bearing carries marginally more direct register, while at the older Anciens Brugeois patrician evenings of Bruges the receiving-line peer-discipline has retained the same composed brevity across post-war generations.

### Q3: Le Déjeuner Professionnel (The Working Lunch)

**Scenario:** At a working lunch of six at Castor & Pollux in Antwerp — three senior commercial-elite figures, two peer-Commandeurs, and the young Cavalier of twenty-eight and young Demoiselle of twenty-six who are both junior at the firm. The lunch is substantive: a cross-jurisdictional commercial question with senior architectural opening. The Cavalier and Demoiselle are seated diagonally across from each other; the senior figures are observing both juniors as the firm's lateral peer-cohort. The next forty minutes calibrate whether the lateral peer-bearing operates at composed neutrality across the working lunch — neither cross-junior conversation that would signal lateral familiarity to the senior cohort, nor over-formal lateral distance that would itself surface as awareness of the senior gaze.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors operate at the same calibrated junior register independently — the Cavalier defers to the senior commercial-elite figure for wine selection, orders lightly, contributes substantively only when the senior architecture has explicitly opened the moment; the Demoiselle calibrates equivalently. When the lateral peer-engagement arises naturally — the senior commercial-elite figure asks the two juniors a question that frames them as the firm's lateral cohort — both parties respond as composed peer-substantive contributors rather than through cross-junior register or through avoidance of the lateral frame. The Cavalier may defer briefly to the Demoiselle's specific knowledge ("the recent regulatory shift falls more in Margaux's substantive area"); the Demoiselle may defer comparably to the Cavalier's ("the cross-jurisdictional question Pierre worked on at Madrid"). The lateral substantive deference operates within the senior-observed frame as composed peer-cohort bearing rather than as cross-junior personal acquaintance.

*The discipline is the joint operation of composed neutral lateral peer-bearing across the working lunch — both juniors visible to the senior cohort as the firm's lateral peer-architecture rather than as cross-junior acquaintance. The substantive lateral deference signals composed reading of each other's substantive areas; the senior commercial-elite figures read the calibrated bearing as the firm's twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel rather than as personal-register acquaintance overlaying the working frame.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same lateral calibration with brief composed substantive cross-exchange when the senior commercial-elite figures explicitly invite the juniors to develop a substantive thread between them — appropriate when the senior frame has explicitly opened the lateral substantive moment within the working frame.

*The contemporary refinement when senior invitation explicitly opens the lateral substantive frame; the cross-exchange operates within composed peer-substantive register, never elaborated into cross-junior personal warmth.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Develop conversational thread between the Cavalier and the Demoiselle that the senior figures register as cross-junior personal warmth; defer to one another in playful register that converts substantive deference into lateral familiarity-display; pre-empt the senior commercial-elite figures' substantive opening through cross-junior bridge; consume more wine than the senior figures' Tempo permits while engaged with each other's lateral conversation; over-correct through visible non-engagement that surfaces the lateral peer-discipline as performance; or lean across the table or angle bodies toward each other in a way the senior cohort registers as personal-register surfacing.

*All six fail. The cross-junior thread is "Flirt Lunch-Surface" — the visible surfacing of lateral peer-warmth into working frame the senior commercial-elite reads precisely. The playful deference is "Cross-Substantive Display" — the conversion of composed substantive deference into lateral familiarity-performance. The bridge pre-emption is "Lateral Pre-emption" — the breach of senior architectural-opening through cross-junior coordination. The wine-Tempo bleed is "Over-Formal Lunch-Stiff" — wait, the wine-Tempo bleed is more accurately "Cross Wine-Tempo" but let me fold this differently — the non-engagement is "Senior-Observed Posture-Drift" — the over-correcting visible distance that surfaces awareness of the senior gaze. The body-angling is "Lateral Body-Angle Drift" — the physical orientation toward the lateral peer that the senior commercial-elite reads as lateral peer-discipline uninternalised.*

**Historical Context:** Le Déjeuner Professionnel for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Antwerp Diamond District commercial-elite working-lunch tradition and at the Avenue Louise senior-firm partner-lunches of Brussels, where the senior commercial-elite cohort has continuously calibrated lateral peer-juniors across post-war generations. The discipline operates equivalently in the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp foundation-circles: at Brussels working lunches the lateral bearing carries marginally more formal register, while at the Ghent patriciaat working lunches the calibration runs slower with additional cultural-substantive register.

### Q4: Tempo Soutenu (Course-Pacing under Conversation)

**Scenario:** At a dinner of fourteen at a private residence in Lasne hosted by a senior-couple foundation patron, the young Cavalier of twenty-nine and the young Demoiselle of twenty-seven are seated near each other — the Cavalier directly across from the Demoiselle's neighbour, the Demoiselle two places to the Cavalier's right. Mid-fish course a substantive conversation has emerged about the European foundation-governance question; both juniors have substantive views from professional formation. The senior Châtelaine hostess is at the head of the table; her gaze sweeps the table at calibrated intervals. The next four minutes calibrate whether the lateral peer-bearing under conversational pressure operates at the same calibrated junior register independently rather than as cross-junior coordination across the table-architecture.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors maintain the Tempo-discipline independently — eating-rhythm matched to the slowest senior diner, cutlery in calibrated centre-cross resting-position before contributing, the half-second pause to swallow before speaking. When contributing to the substantive thread, both calibrate brevity and questioning register at the junior level. The lateral cross-table engagement is preserved as composed parallel substantive contribution: the Cavalier addresses the senior figures across his end of the table, the Demoiselle addresses the senior figures across her end; if their substantive views connect across the table-architecture, the cross-link is offered as composed substantive contribution to the senior frame rather than as cross-junior conversational thread. Eye-contact during contribution is calibrated to the senior figures rather than locked onto the lateral peer; the lateral acknowledgement of the cross-table substantive resonance is brief and composed — a composed brief glance at the natural pause rather than sustained engagement that would convert cross-table dynamics into cross-junior duet.

*The discipline is the joint operation of independent calibrated junior Tempo with absorbed lateral substantive-resonance — both juniors visible to the senior Châtelaine hostess at the head of the table as twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel rather than as cross-junior conversational architecture. The independent calibrated Tempo signals each junior's individual formation; the absorbed lateral resonance signals composed mutual substantive recognition without conversion into cross-junior duet.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same lateral calibration with one brief composed direct cross-table contribution when the senior frame has explicitly opened the lateral substantive moment — the Demoiselle's brief direct response to the Cavalier's substantive contribution within the table's running thread — appropriate when the senior Châtelaine hostess or another senior has framed the cross-table connection within the substantive frame.

*The contemporary refinement when senior framing has opened the cross-table substantive moment; the brief direct contribution operates within the senior frame, never elaborated into cross-junior duet.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Develop conversational thread directly between the Cavalier and the Demoiselle across the table-architecture that the senior Châtelaine hostess registers as cross-junior duet; lock eye-contact during contributions onto the lateral peer rather than onto the senior figures the contribution addresses; speak with food still in the mouth while engaged with each other's substantive thread; lay the cutlery down dramatically to engage the cross-table dynamic; or surface the lateral peer-acquaintance through the smile-extension across the table that the senior Châtelaine hostess reads as personal-register exchange overlaying the substantive frame.

*All five fail. The cross-table duet is "Cross-Junior Duet Push" — the visible cross-table thread that the senior Châtelaine hostess registers as compositional gap of formed lateral peer-discipline. The eye-contact lock is "Flirt Mid-Bite" — the visible peer-anchoring during contributions that surfaces personal-register through cross-table eye-contact. The food-in-mouth contribution is "Cross Mid-Speech" — the audibly compromised speech while engaged with the lateral peer-substantive thread. The cutlery drop is "Cutlery Cross-Drop" — the displacement of composed Tempo into cross-junior engagement-display. The smile-extension is "Senior-Observed Catch-Up" — the visible cross-table warmth that the senior Châtelaine hostess at the head reads precisely.*

**Historical Context:** The Tempo Bourguignon under conversational pressure for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Brabant Wallon foundation-evening tradition and at the Brussels patrician townhouse multi-generational dinners, where the senior Châtelaine hostess cohort has continuously calibrated the lateral peer-bearing of younger generations under conversational pressure. The convention carries calibrated rhythms across the francophone and Flemish elite-registers: at the Antwerp commercial-elite dinners the lateral Tempo bears marginally more direct conversational pace, while at the Ghent patriciaat dinners of the Korenlei tradition the lateral Tempo runs marginally slower with additional contemplative register.

### Q5: Registre du Service (The Service-Staff Register)

**Scenario:** At a private dinner of twelve at Comme Chez Soi, the young Cavalier of twenty-six and the young Demoiselle of twenty-five are seated as adjacent diners near the centre of the table; both require additional bread and water mid-meal during the same course-pause. The waiter approaches between them; the senior Châtelaine across the table is observing. The next twenty seconds calibrate whether the lateral peer-bearing during a shared service-encounter operates at composed independent junior register rather than as coordinated cross-junior encounter that would surface as lateral familiarity to the senior cohort.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors address the waiter independently with the calibrated junior register: the Cavalier offers his brief composed request first as the waiter arrives at his side ("Un peu de pain, s'il vous plaît, et de l'eau plate"), the Demoiselle offers her parallel brief composed request as the waiter turns to her side. No cross-coordination ("we both need..."); no lateral acknowledgement of the parallel needs through brief glance to one another that would surface as cross-junior coordination; no extended dialogue with the waiter from either junior. The composed parallel independent service-encounters are visible to the senior Châtelaine across the table as twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel rather than as cross-junior coordinated request.

*The discipline is the joint independent operation of the service-staff register — both juniors address the waiter at the calibrated junior middle-register without cross-coordination that would convert two parallel encounters into single cross-junior moment. The composed independence preserves each junior's individual service-staff register; the senior Châtelaine across the table reads the parallel composed bearings as twin formations.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same parallel independent service-encounter with brief composed cross-acknowledgement to the waiter — the Cavalier's request followed by composed nod toward the Demoiselle: "et la même chose pour Margaux?" — appropriate only when the waiter has reached the Cavalier and the Demoiselle's parallel need has been visibly evident through her empty bread plate, and only when the lateral acquaintance is itself composed enough that the brief named reference does not surface as personal-register.

*The contemporary refinement when proximity makes the brief named reference efficient; the reference is composed and brief, never elaborated into cross-junior conversational register with the staff.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Coordinate the request through cross-junior conversation ("we both need bread, no?"); engage in lateral commentary about each other's preferences for the waiter's hearing; offer one comprehensive request that bundles both juniors' needs through the Cavalier's authority over the lateral encounter; thank the waiter through cross-junior coordinated acknowledgement; or engage in extended apologetic-cross softening that signals discomfort with the parallel encounter.

*All five fail. The cross-junior coordination is "Cross Solicitous-Drift" — the conversion of two parallel encounters into single cross-junior moment the senior Châtelaine across the table reads precisely as compositional gap. The lateral commentary is "Cross Imperious-Drift" — the visible cross-junior conversational register inappropriate to the staff-encounter frame. The Cavalier's bundled request is "Bundled-Request Drift" — the false cross-junior authority that the Demoiselle's own service-encounter cannot warrant from the Cavalier's side. The cross-acknowledgement is "Cross Volume-Thanks" — the bilateral effusion at table-volume the senior Châtelaine reads as twin compositional gaps. The apologetic-cross is "Cross Apology-Cascade" — the bilateral softening that signals discomfort with the parallel encounter and registers as lateral peer-discipline uninternalised.*

**Historical Context:** The service-staff register for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the multi-generation establishment tradition — Comme Chez Soi across the Wynants ownership since 1926, La Villa Lorraine at the Bois de la Cambre since 1972, La Maison du Cygne in the older Brussels Grand-Place tradition. The discipline operates equivalently in the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp gastronomic-establishment circles: at the Antwerp commercial-elite establishments the lateral parallel register operates with marginally more direct register, while at the Liège Cercle dinners the parallel register carries additional warmth in keeping with the Walloon convivial tradition.

### Q6: La Calibration Latérale (The Lateral Peer-Bearing in Senior-Observed Cluster)

**Scenario:** At a foundation evening at a residence in Hoeilaart, the young Cavalier of twenty-eight and the young Demoiselle of twenty-six find themselves in a cluster of four with two senior Patriarche figures. The two juniors and the two seniors stand in roughly square configuration; the two seniors are conversing on the foundation-strategy question. The senior Châtelaines are at adjacent clusters; one of them is the wife of one of the senior Patriarche figures in the cluster and her gaze is calibrated to the four-cluster periodically. The next several minutes — perhaps the cluster will hold for ten or fifteen minutes — calibrate whether the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-bearing has internalised La Calibration Latérale, the discipline of standing in cluster with the lateral peer under sustained senior-observation.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors operate at composed neutral peer-bearing toward the senior conversation: bodies angled toward the two senior Patriarche figures rather than toward each other, eyes attentive to the running thread, contributions offered briefly only when the senior frame has opened. The lateral peer-acknowledgement is preserved through composed minimal cross-recognition: a brief composed glance to the lateral peer when one of the senior figures has just made a substantive point that resonates with shared professional context, the brief glance returned with composed brief acknowledgement, the gaze returning to the senior figures within the same breath. Neither junior turns the body toward the other; neither extends the lateral acknowledgement beyond the brief composed glance; neither surfaces personal-register or warmth through facial register. The calibrated lateral peer-bearing operates as composed parallel attention with absorbed brief lateral resonance — the senior Patriarche's wife at the adjacent cluster reads the calibrated bearing as twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel under sustained senior gaze.

*The discipline is "La Calibration Latérale" — the principle that the lateral peer-bearing in senior-observed clusters operates as composed parallel attention rather than as either cross-junior coordination or as visible lateral distance that surfaces awareness of the senior gaze. The discipline carries five-fold weight: avoid flirt-drift register, avoid over-formal drift, avoid familiarity-cascade, avoid diffident-distance, avoid the surfacing of awareness of the senior gaze through over-corrective bearing. The composed parallel attention with absorbed brief lateral resonance is the formed lateral peer-discipline; the senior Patriarche's wife at the adjacent cluster reads the calibrated bearing as the most diagnostic moment confirming twin junior formations operating in parallel calibration rather than as cross-junior personal acquaintance overlaying the cluster-frame.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same composed parallel attention with one brief composed direct lateral exchange when the senior frame has explicitly opened the lateral substantive moment — the senior Patriarche figure asking the two juniors a substantive question that explicitly addresses them as the foundation's lateral cohort — appropriate when the senior frame has explicitly framed the lateral substantive engagement.

*The contemporary refinement when senior framing has opened the lateral substantive frame; the brief direct exchange operates within composed peer-substantive register, never elaborated into cross-junior personal warmth.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Allow the body-orientation to drift toward the lateral peer through subtle three-quarter angle that the senior Patriarche's wife reads as flirt-drift; over-correct the orientation toward stiff parallel facing-away that surfaces awareness of senior gaze; surface lateral familiarity through the brief shared smile at a senior anecdotal moment that converts cluster-frame into cross-junior personal-register; develop substantive sub-thread between the lateral peers that displaces the senior conversation; or retreat into visible lateral distance that itself signals cross-junior peer-acquaintance through over-corrected bearing.

*All five fail. The body-drift is "Flirt-Drift Lateral" — the visible orientation that the senior Patriarche's wife at the adjacent cluster reads precisely as compositional gap of formed lateral peer-discipline. The stiff over-correction is "Over-Formal Lateral" — the visible orientation that itself surfaces awareness of senior gaze and registers as lateral peer-discipline uninternalised. The shared smile is "Lateral Smile-Surface" — the cross-junior facial register at the senior anecdotal moment that converts cluster-architecture into cross-junior exchange. The substantive sub-thread is "Lateral Substantive-Hyper-Push" — the cross-junior conversation that displaces the senior frame. The visible lateral distance is "Senior-Gaze Posture-Failure" — the over-corrected bearing that signals lateral peer-discipline uninternalised through the visible attempt to perform peer-discipline.*

**Historical Context:** La Calibration Latérale is preserved at the Brabant Wallon foundation-evening tradition at Hoeilaart, La Hulpe, Lasne, and Genval, and at the Brussels patrician townhouse foundation evenings, where the senior Patriarche cohort and the senior Châtelaine cohort have continuously calibrated the lateral peer-bearing of younger generations under sustained senior gaze across post-war generations of Belgian elite formation. The convention runs in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp foundation-circles: at the Antwerp commercial-elite foundation evenings the lateral peer-bearing operates with marginally more direct register, while at the older Anciens Brugeois patrician evenings of Bruges the lateral peer-discipline has retained the same composed parallel-attention across centuries of preserved practice.

### Q7: Le Protocole de Présentation (The Introduction Protocol)

**Scenario:** At a foundation gala held at a country residence near Spa, the young Cavalier of twenty-seven stands in conversation with a senior Patriarche figure when the young Demoiselle of twenty-five approaches; the senior Patriarche does not know her, though the Cavalier and the Demoiselle have established professional acquaintance. The Cavalier must introduce them. The next forty seconds calibrate whether the lateral peer-introduction has been internalised — the discipline of introducing the lateral peer to the senior figure with composed neutral substantive register rather than as personal-acquaintance reference.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Cavalier pauses the running conversation cleanly; introduces the senior Patriarche first by full name and substantive standing; introduces the Demoiselle by full name and her own substantive standing — anchored in her professional formation rather than in the Cavalier's relation to her, the substantive standing the Demoiselle herself would offer rather than the personal-register acquaintance that prior foundation-overlaps have generated. "Madame [Surname], may I introduce Mademoiselle [Surname], counsel at [firm name] specialising in the institutional-question." The bridge connects through the Demoiselle's substantive area rather than through the lateral peer-acquaintance; the Cavalier withdraws by half a step. The Demoiselle calibrates her acknowledgement to composed neutral substantive register that operates as the Cavalier has framed her — substantive professional rather than lateral peer-acquaintance. The composed lateral peer-introduction operates as architecture rather than as personal-acquaintance bridge.

*The discipline is the joint operation of the lateral peer-introduction at composed neutral substantive register — the Cavalier introduces the Demoiselle by her own substantive standing rather than through reference to lateral peer-acquaintance; the Demoiselle receives the introduction within the substantive frame the Cavalier has constructed rather than surfacing the lateral acquaintance. The senior Patriarche reads the composed lateral peer-introduction as the marker of formed lateral peer-discipline that has internalised the principle that introductions establish architecture rather than reveal acquaintance.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same calibrated introduction with the Cavalier's substantive bridge expanding into a single composed sentence when the substantive overlap genuinely advances the new conversation — appropriate when the substantive bridge serves the introduction rather than the lateral peer-acquaintance.

*The contemporary refinement when substantive bridging warrants brief expansion; the addition is composed and brief, never elaborated into reference to the lateral peer-acquaintance.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Introduce the Demoiselle through reference to the lateral peer-acquaintance ("an old friend from the foundation-evenings"); surface the personal-register through warmth-extension during the introduction sequence; bridge the introduction through prior shared lateral-context rather than through the Demoiselle's own substantive standing; persist in the introduction-frame through extended biographical elaboration drawn from lateral acquaintance; or fail to register the senior Patriarche's structural precedence through the brief verbal sequence.

*All five fail. The lateral acquaintance reference is "Cross Mediation-Display" — the conversion of substantive introduction into lateral peer-acquaintance reference that the senior Patriarche reads precisely as compositional gap. The warmth-extension is "Cross Bridge-Elaboration" — the visible surfacing of personal-register during the introduction sequence. The lateral-context bridge is "Cross Architecture-Substitute" — the substantive standing displaced by lateral peer-acquaintance reference. The persistent elaboration is "Cross Persistent-Mediator" — the visible refusal to withdraw conversational priority. The senior bypass is "Cross Precedence-Slip" — the failure of structural verbal sequence through informal lateral-register.*

**Historical Context:** Le Protocole de Présentation for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Walloon foundation-gala tradition at Spa and at the Brabant Wallon foundation-evening tradition, where the senior Patriarche cohort has continuously calibrated the lateral peer-introduction across post-war generations. The discipline runs with calibrated rhythms across the francophone and Flemish elite-introductions: at the Antwerp commercial-elite introductions the protocol operates with marginally more direct register, while at the Ghent patriciaat introductions of the Korenlei the protocol carries additional cultural-substantive bridging in keeping with the Ghent intellectual tradition.

### Q8: Lecture des Salles (Cross-Cluster Reading)

**Scenario:** At a multi-table dinner-evening at the Cercle Munster — six tables of eight, the young Cavalier of twenty-six seated at one of the smaller clusters with a senior associate and two peer-Cavaliers, the young Demoiselle of twenty-four seated at a different table at the far end with three Châtelaines and her senior partner. During a course-pause the Cavalier sees the Demoiselle across the room; her gaze briefly catches his. The next fifteen seconds calibrate whether the cross-table lateral peer-recognition operates within the composed brief register that signals professional-acquaintance recognition without surfacing as lateral peer-personal exchange.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Hold the eye-contact for the composed brief moment — long enough to be unmistakable as recognition, brief enough to be calibrated; offer the faint composed inclination of the head — the same inclination the Cavalier would offer any peer-Cavalier across the room; allow the gaze to return to the immediate cluster within the natural rhythm of conversational attention. The Demoiselle calibrates her return-recognition equivalently — brief composed inclination, the gaze returning to her own cluster's running thread. No prolonged eye-contact that would convert brief recognition into cross-table lateral exchange the senior Châtelaines at multiple tables would register precisely; no smile-warmth that would surface personal-register; no glass-lift in cross-table salute. The composed brief mutual inclination operates as professional-acquaintance recognition absorbed into the multi-table architecture.

*The discipline is the joint operation of cross-table lateral peer-recognition at composed brief register — both parties register the cross-table moment without surfacing the lateral peer-acquaintance through extended recognition or through warmth-register that the senior Châtelaines at the multi-table evening would read precisely. The composed brief mutual inclination is the formed lateral peer-discipline; the calibrated brevity preserves both clusters' substantive integrity.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same brief acknowledgement followed by composed brief approach during the natural intermission between courses if the cross-table layout permits — five seconds at the Demoiselle's table, brief composed acknowledgement of her senior partner and the Châtelaines at her table, no extended lateral exchange — appropriate when the inter-course architecture permits brief direct presence and the lateral acquaintance is genuinely substantive enough to warrant brief direct acknowledgement that does not displace the cluster-architecture.

*The contemporary refinement permitting calibrated brief intermission-presence; the brief approach honours the senior partner and the Châtelaines at the Demoiselle's table rather than focusing on the lateral peer-recognition.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Maintain extended cross-table eye-contact that surfaces personal-register; raise the glass across the room in cross-junior salute; gesture or wave; rotate the torso fully toward the other table; abandon one's own cluster mid-course to approach the other table; surface a smile that the senior Châtelaines at multiple tables read as flirt-drift across the multi-table architecture; or pretend not to have seen the eye-contact in over-formal denial.

*All seven fail. The extended hold is "Cross Eye-Lock" — the conversion of brief recognition into cross-table lateral exchange the senior Châtelaines register precisely as compositional gap. The cross-room glass is "Cross Glass-Salute" — the displacement of brief register through ceremonial cross-junior salute. The gesture is "Cross Hand-Wave" — the breach of multi-table architecture through visible cross-room communication. The torso-rotation is "Cross Cluster-Pivot" — the visible turn that signals abandoned cluster-engagement. The mid-course approach is "Cross Course-Cut" — the breach of one's own cluster's conversational frame for cross-table presence. The smile-surface is "Cross-Junior Smile-Surface" — the warmth-register the senior Châtelaines across multiple tables read as flirt-drift. The over-formal denial is "Cross Recognition-Refusal" — the visible non-recognition that itself signals awareness of the lateral peer-acquaintance.*

**Historical Context:** The cross-table reading for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Cercle Munster and Cercle Royal Gaulois multi-table evenings of Brussels, where the senior Châtelaine cohort has continuously calibrated the lateral peer-cross-table register across post-war generations. The convention operates equivalently in the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp clubland traditions: at the Antwerp Engelse Conversatiekring multi-table evenings the cross-cluster register carries marginally more direct register, while at the older Anciens Brugeois patrician evenings of Bruges the register operates with the same calibrated brevity across centuries of preserved practice.

### Q9: La Discipline de Dégustation (The Tasting Discipline)

**Scenario:** At a Brabant Wallon residence cellar-tasting at Genval hosted by an older relative of one of the junior cohort — six guests around a tasting table, including two senior figures, one peer-Commandeur, and the young Cavalier of twenty-eight and young Demoiselle of twenty-six who are both at junior-formation in their wine-knowledge. The host has selected three vintage bottles. The Cavalier and the Demoiselle have both followed wine-formation independently and recognise some elements of the second bottle's domaine. The next thirty minutes calibrate whether the lateral peer-bearing during the tasting operates at composed independent junior-tasting register rather than as cross-junior tasting-coordination that would surface as lateral pair-bearing to the senior collector and his wife.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors operate at the same calibrated junior-tasting register independently — the swirl brief and composed without performative depth, the nose taken without theatrical inhalation, the sip held briefly without performative palate-display, the brief composed assent to each pour. Neither cross-references the other's tasting-rhythm; neither offers brief lateral observations between pours; neither develops cross-junior wine-conversation in undertone during the tasting-thread. When the host opens substantive discussion among the senior collectors, both juniors listen with composed attention; if the host directs a question to one of them, the response operates within the host's frame anchored in shared appreciation rather than in lateral peer-tasting-formation that would convert the response into cross-junior coordinated commentary. The senior collector and his wife read the parallel composed independent tasting-discipline as twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel rather than as cross-junior tasting-pair.

*The discipline is the joint operation of independent calibrated junior-tasting register — both juniors maintain individual wine-formation withholding without cross-junior coordination that would convert two parallel withholdings into single cross-junior tasting-architecture. The composed independence preserves each junior's individual wine-discipline; the senior collector's wife reads the parallel composed bearings as twin formations.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same parallel independent tasting-discipline with one brief composed cross-acknowledgement when the host explicitly directs a substantive question to both juniors — appropriate when the host's invitation explicitly opens the lateral substantive moment within the tasting-frame.

*The contemporary refinement when host invitation has explicitly opened the lateral substantive frame; the brief cross-acknowledgement operates within composed peer-substantive register, never elaborated into cross-junior tasting-coordination.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Cross-reference the lateral peer's tasting-rhythm through brief glance during pour-progression; offer brief lateral observations on the second domaine in undertone between pours; develop cross-junior wine-conversation that signals twin wine-formation; coordinate withholdings through visible cross-junior eye-contact at moments when both recognise the second bottle's significance; or surface lateral peer-recognition of shared wine-knowledge through the calibrated composed-smile that the senior collector's wife reads as cross-junior tasting-coordination.

*All five fail. The cross-glance during pours is "Cross Domaine-Display" — the conversion of independent tasting-discipline into cross-junior tasting-coordination the senior collector's wife reads precisely. The undertone observations is "Cross Voice-Pitch" — the lateral commentary that surfaces cross-junior tasting-architecture. The cross-conversation is "Cross Cellar-Inquiry" — the visible coordination of cross-junior wine-formation. The withholding-coordination eye-contact is "Cross Possession-Reference" — the cross-junior acknowledgement of shared recognition that converts parallel withholdings into coordinated discipline. The composed-smile recognition is "Cross Connoisseur-Swirl" — the bilateral facial register of shared wine-knowledge that the senior collector's wife reads as cross-junior tasting-pair.*

**Historical Context:** La Discipline de Dégustation for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Brabant Wallon residential cellar-tasting tradition at Genval, La Hulpe, and Rixensart, where the senior collector cohort has continuously calibrated lateral junior-pair tasting-discipline across post-war generations. The convention runs across the francophone and Flemish elite-tasting traditions in calibrated form: at the Antwerp commercial-elite tastings the lateral parallel discipline operates with marginally more direct conversational register, while at the older Brussels gastronomic-establishment tastings at La Villa Lorraine and Bon-Bon the register carries the same calibrated parallel restraint across decades of preserved practice.

### Q10: Le Départ Mesuré (The Departure Calibration)

**Scenario:** At the conclusion of a four-hour evening at a Ghent foundation residence near the Korenlei, the young Cavalier of twenty-seven and young Demoiselle of twenty-five rise within the natural departure-rhythm — they had arrived independently and will depart independently. The post-coffee moment has settled and they happen to rise at adjacent moments in the cohort's departure-rhythm. The next ten minutes calibrate whether the lateral peer-departure operates at composed independent junior register rather than as coordinated cross-junior departure that would surface as lateral pair-bearing to the senior Châtelaine hostess.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Both juniors operate the departure-architecture independently: each rises at their own calibrated third-or-fourth turn moment, approaches the senior Châtelaine hostess separately at the salon doorway, offers the composed warm farewell with the substantive farewell-remark naming a specific moment of the evening, departs after composed brief farewells to the senior partner and the immediate cluster. Neither coordinates the rise-timing with the other; neither approaches the salon doorway in cross-junior parallel; neither departs the entrance hall together in coordinated rhythm. If both happen to be at the entrance simultaneously during coat-collection, the brief composed nod operates as the same composed brief register offered to any peer at the same moment — no cross-junior conversation, no coordinated step toward the door, no smile-warmth that would surface lateral peer-personal departure-coordination. Each operates the departure as composed independent junior-architecture; the senior Châtelaine hostess reads the parallel composed departures as twin junior formations operating in calibrated parallel.

*The discipline is the joint operation of independent calibrated junior-departure — both juniors operate the departure-architecture without cross-junior coordination that would convert two parallel departures into single cross-junior pair-departure. The composed independence preserves each junior's individual departure-discipline; the senior Châtelaine hostess reads the parallel composed bearings as twin formations rather than as cross-junior pair leaving together.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same parallel independent departure with brief composed acknowledgement at the entrance hall during coat-collection if the moment naturally aligns — composed brief nod, no verbal cross-exchange, the parallel departure-architecture preserved through the entrance — appropriate when the simultaneity is natural rather than coordinated.

*The contemporary refinement permitting calibrated brief acknowledgement at the entrance; the brief moment is composed and parallel rather than coordinated, the independent departure-architecture preserved.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Coordinate the rise-timing with the lateral peer through cross-glance during the post-coffee moment; approach the salon doorway in cross-junior parallel that signals coordinated departure; engage the lateral peer in conversation at the entrance hall during coat-collection; depart the residence together in coordinated step-rhythm; offer the senior Châtelaine hostess the cross-junior coordinated farewell that the senior reads precisely as cross-junior pair-bearing; or surface lateral peer-personal register through warmth-extended farewell at the entrance.

*All six fail. The cross-glance rise-timing is "Cross Skip-Farewell" — the conversion of independent departure into coordinated cross-junior departure the senior Châtelaine hostess registers precisely as compositional gap. The cross-junior parallel approach is "Cross Generic-Effusion" — the visible coordinated departure-architecture inappropriate to lateral peer-discipline. The entrance-hall conversation is "Cross Doorway-Anchor" — the breach of independent departure-architecture through cross-junior conversation. The coordinated step-rhythm is "Cross Re-Entry" — the visible cross-junior coordination through the threshold the senior Châtelaine hostess reads as lateral pair-bearing. The cross-junior farewell is "Cross Salon-Coat" — the bilateral coordinated farewell at the architectural close. The warmth-extended farewell is "Cross Staff-Praise" — the surfacing of personal-register at the entrance that converts independent departures into cross-junior personal-departure pair.*

**Historical Context:** Le Départ Mesuré for the lateral Cavalier-Demoiselle peer-engagement is preserved at the Ghent foundation tradition of the Korenlei patriciaat and at the older Brabant Wallon residential evenings, where the senior Châtelaine hostess cohort has continuously calibrated the lateral peer-departure across post-war generations. The convention persists in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp departure-traditions: at the Antwerp foundation evenings the lateral parallel departure carries marginally more direct register in keeping with Antwerp commercial confidence, while at the Liège Cercle bourgeois evenings the parallel departure runs marginally warmer in keeping with the Walloon convivial register.

Belgium — Phase 1 — Pillar 3: The Table — Level 2: The Practitioner — Cross-Demographic: Demoiselle ↔ Cavalier (V19-30 with M19-30, Demoiselle-Frame Initiated)

*Focus: The applied semi-public architecture calibrated to the lateral peer-engagement initiated from the young Demoiselle's frame — joining the cluster in motion at a Brussels Sablon foundation reception where the Demoiselle is the active approacher (L'Abordage), the joint-arrival at the receiving-line where the Demoiselle precedes by half a step (Calibration des Hôtes), the Demoiselle-convened Sea Grill working-lunch with the Cavalier as junior peer-attendee (Le Déjeuner Professionnel), the calibrated composed peer-bearing where the Demoiselle's frame initiates the lateral architecture (La Calibration Composée), the introduction-protocol where the Demoiselle introduces the Cavalier to a senior figure (Le Protocole de Présentation), the withheld lateral peer-formation when the Demoiselle has introduced the Cavalier into her uncle's Stavelot cellar-tasting (La Discipline de Dégustation). The codes elevate beyond the foundational L1 register into the higher-stakes practice of female-initiated peer-engagement under senior gaze at Royal Yacht Club Belgium multi-table evenings, the Square Marie-Louise diplomatic Brussels foundation-galas, the Antwerp Engelse Conversatiekring senior-cohort dinners, and the multi-day Belgian elite calendar where the Demoiselle's lateral peer-frame must operate without surfacing forward-female register or compensatory over-modesty. The senior Châtelaines and the senior Patriarche register both read the calibrated bearing as the marker of formation that has internalised the discipline of female-initiated peer-engagement — neither forward-female push nor compensatory under-claiming surfaces — the composed lateral peer-bearing where the Demoiselle's frame opens the architecture and the Cavalier's bearing reciprocates within it.*

### Q1: L'Abordage (The Reception Approach)

**Scenario:** At a foundation reception held in the Sablon townhouse of one of the older patrician families, the young Demoiselle of twenty-six arrives mid-evening with a flute of champagne accepted at the entrance and recognises the young Cavalier of twenty-eight in a cluster of three near the high windows — he is in conversation with two senior Patriarche figures. The Demoiselle and the Cavalier have established professional acquaintance through prior foundation-overlaps. The senior Châtelaine wife of one of the senior Patriarche figures is at the adjacent cluster within sightline. The next thirty seconds calibrate whether the Demoiselle-initiated L'Abordage operates within the lateral peer-discipline that the senior gaze reads precisely — without surfacing forward-female register and equally without compensatory over-modest register that would surface awareness of the gender-dynamic before its resolution.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Demoiselle approaches the cluster on the calibrated diagonal — the body angled three-quarters toward the cluster, the flute held at the lower-chest register, the eyes available without the lowered-gaze register that signals junior-female deference and equally without the held-gaze register that would direct attention onto the Cavalier as cluster-anchor. Pause at the calibrated four-paces distance — half a pace further than the established practitioner would hold, the additional measured deference of the junior-female register. Wait for the senior Patriarche figures to extend the inclusion-gesture; never solicit through eye-contact persistence with the Cavalier that would convert cluster-entry into lateral peer-arrival rather than composed substantive approach. The Cavalier in turn calibrates his recognition to the composed brief register he would offer any peer joining the cluster — composed brief inclination of the head, no warmth-extension, no smile-anticipation, no positional-shift toward the arriving peer. The composed mutual approach-and-reception absorbed into the cluster-architecture operates as the formed lateral peer-discipline.

*The discipline is the joint operation of the Demoiselle-initiated approach at composed neutral substantive register — the Demoiselle's L'Abordage must avoid both the forward-female register (eye-contact persistence with Cavalier, body-angling toward Cavalier as cluster-anchor) and the compensatory over-modest register (lowered gaze that surfaces gender-awareness, hesitant approach-rhythm that surfaces awareness of the senior gaze before its own resolution); the Cavalier's reciprocation must not surface the lateral acquaintance through warmth-extension or positional-shift. The composed substantive approach absorbed into the cluster-architecture is the formed lateral peer-discipline; the senior Châtelaine wife at the adjacent cluster reads the calibrated bearing as the diagnostic moment confirming twin formations operating in calibrated parallel where the Demoiselle's frame opens the architectural moment and the Cavalier's reciprocation operates within it.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same calibrated approach with a brief substantive contribution from the Demoiselle once admission has been granted — the brief composed remark explicitly addressing the senior Patriarche figures rather than the Cavalier, anchored in the substantive thread the senior figures are developing — appropriate when the substantive standing of the Demoiselle has been recognised in prior foundation-evenings.

*The contemporary refinement when substantive contribution from the Demoiselle is welcomed; the contribution honours the senior Patriarche figures' authority over the running thread and explicitly does not address the Cavalier as primary interlocutor.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Approach the cluster with eye-contact pattern that solicits the Cavalier's recognition through sustained attention; allow the body-angle to drift toward the Cavalier as cluster-anchor; surface the brief composed-smile of recognition that the senior Châtelaine wife at the adjacent cluster reads as forward-female register; the Cavalier responds with warmth-extension or positional-shift that confirms the cross-junior recognition; or retreat into compensatory lowered-gaze register that surfaces awareness of the gender-dynamic and registers as compositional gap.

*All five fail. The eye-contact solicitation is "Forward-Female Approach" — the conversion of substantive cluster-entry into Cavalier-anchored approach that the senior Châtelaine wife reads precisely as compositional gap. The body-angle drift is "Demoiselle-Edge Drift" — the visible orientation toward the Cavalier as cluster-anchor that displaces the substantive cluster-architecture. The composed-smile recognition is "Pre-Acceptance Smile" — the warmth-register before the inclusion-gesture has been extended that surfaces lateral acquaintance into the approach-rhythm. The Cavalier's warmth-extension is "Cavalier-Reciprocation Drift" — the visible reception that confirms the cross-junior recognition. The lowered-gaze retreat is "Compensatory Over-Modesty" — the visible junior-female deference that surfaces awareness of the gender-dynamic and registers as Demoiselle-formation gap.*

**Historical Context:** L'Abordage for the Demoiselle-initiated lateral peer-engagement is preserved at the Brussels Sablon foundation receptions and the Avenue Louise senior-firm receptions, where the senior Châtelaine cohort has continuously calibrated the lateral peer-bearing of younger generations across post-war generations of female-initiating Demoiselle formation. The convention runs in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp foundation-circles: at the Antwerp Engelse Conversatiekring receptions the Demoiselle-initiated approach operates with marginally more direct register, while at the Liège Cercle bourgeois receptions the female-initiated rhythm carries additional convivial warmth without surrendering the calibrated peer-discipline.

### Q2: Calibration des Hôtes (Multi-Host Calibration)

**Scenario:** Arriving at the same moment at a foundation co-hosting evening at a country residence in La Hulpe, the young Demoiselle of twenty-five and the young Cavalier of twenty-seven encounter each other at the threshold of the entrance hall — they are about to enter the receiving-line in immediate sequence. They have established professional acquaintance from prior evenings; the Châtelaines at the receiving-line are visible just inside. The next twenty seconds calibrate whether the joint-arrival sequence operates as composed independent parallel arrival rather than as cross-junior pair-arrival that would surface to the Châtelaines as lateral peer-couple bearing.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Demoiselle precedes by half a step — the gender-priority traditional in Belgian elite multi-host architecture — the Cavalier's brief composed inclination signalling the deference without verbal exchange that would convert the brief sequence-moment into cross-junior coordination. The Cavalier does not extend his arm, does not gesture-defer with overt motion, does not place his hand at the Demoiselle's lower back as he might in a romantic-coupled register; the composed half-step deferral is signalled through the calibrated brief inclination alone. The Demoiselle proceeds into the receiving-line at composed pace; she does not glance back to the Cavalier, does not pause-at-line-entry to acknowledge his approach, does not signal the joint-arrival to the Châtelaines through the verbal "we have arrived together" register. The Cavalier follows at the calibrated single-step distance — close enough to register as next-in-line, distant enough not to register as pair. The Châtelaines greet them as composed parallel-arrivers, the joint-arrival absorbed into independent parallel architecture.

*The discipline is the joint preservation of independent parallel architecture under joint-arrival — the half-step gender-priority deferral preserves the Belgian elite multi-host tradition without converting the brief deferral-moment into cross-junior coordination; both juniors operate independent parallel bearings even within the shared threshold-moment. The Châtelaines read the calibrated independent parallel arrivals as twin junior formations operating in parallel calibration rather than as cross-junior pair-arriving-together.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same composed parallel arrival with the Demoiselle offering a brief composed verbal acknowledgement of the Cavalier as she steps into the receiving-line — "Pierre" delivered at quiet volume in passing — appropriate when the lateral acquaintance is itself composed enough that the brief named reference does not surface as personal-register inappropriate to the threshold-moment.

*The contemporary refinement when verbal acknowledgement is brief enough to absorb without displacing the parallel-arrival architecture; the named reference operates within composed register, never elaborated into shared-arrival narrative.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Allow the brief sequence-moment to extend into joint-arrival exchange ("after you" with smile); the Cavalier extends his arm or places his hand at the Demoiselle's lower back in romantic-coupled register; the Demoiselle pauses at the line-entry to glance back to the Cavalier in cross-junior coordination; surface the joint-arrival to the Châtelaines through the verbal acknowledgement; or surface the awareness of joint-arrival through over-corrective separation that itself reads as awareness of the cross-junior moment.

*All five fail. The extended exchange is "Pre-Line Glance-Back" — the conversion of brief sequence-moment into cross-junior coordination the Châtelaines register precisely as compositional gap. The romantic-coupled gesture is "Behind-Cavalier Smile-Wait" — the visible cross-junior physical acknowledgement that the Châtelaines read as romantic-coupled bearing inappropriate to the foundation-evening. The pause-glance-back is "Receiving-Line Pause-For-Cavalier" — the visible cross-junior coordination at the line-entry. The verbal joint-arrival surface is "Cross-Line Acknowledgement" — the conversion of independent parallel into cross-junior pair-arrival the Châtelaines register precisely. The over-corrective separation is "Châtelaine-Reading Bypass" — the visible distance that itself surfaces awareness of the cross-junior moment.*

**Historical Context:** The multi-host architecture under joint-arrival for the Demoiselle-Cavalier lateral peer-engagement is preserved at the Brabant Wallon foundation-evening tradition at La Hulpe, Lasne, Genval, and Rixensart, where the senior Châtelaines have continuously calibrated the joint-arrival sequence across post-war generations of Belgian multi-host formation. The convention extends across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp foundation-traditions in calibrated form: at the Antwerp commercial-elite foundation evenings the joint-arrival sequence carries marginally more direct register, while at the older Anciens Brugeois patrician evenings of Bruges the half-step gender-priority architecture has retained the same composed independent-parallel discipline across post-war generations.

### Q3: Le Déjeuner Professionnel (The Working Lunch)

**Scenario:** At a working lunch of six at Sea Grill convened by the Demoiselle of twenty-eight on behalf of her senior partner — the senior partner has asked her to organise the substantive working lunch, including coordinating the establishment booking, the briefing-papers, and the timing logistics. Two senior figures are attending (a senior PATRIARCHE and a peer-Châtelaine), one peer-Commandeur, and the Cavalier of twenty-nine as junior cohort attendee on the matter. The Demoiselle is the convener-junior — formally junior at the table, but with the senior partner's delegated organisational authority. The next forty minutes calibrate whether the Demoiselle's convener-bearing operates at composed delegated-authority register without surfacing as Demoiselle-display, and whether the Cavalier's reciprocal junior-attendee bearing operates without misreading the Demoiselle's convener-frame as lateral peer-coordination.

**A) ✅ Good**

> The Demoiselle operates the convener-functions with composed brief authority that signals delegated organisational standing rather than substantive-rank claim: brief composed direction to the maître d' on the seating, brief composed signal to the senior PATRIARCHE that the substantive working frame is opening, brief composed reference to the prepared briefing-papers when the substantive thread requires the institutional anchor. The substantive contribution from the Demoiselle is calibrated to the delegated-authority register: she opens the substantive thread on behalf of the senior partner, she does not contribute her own substantive views beyond the convener's framing function. The Cavalier reciprocates as composed junior-attendee — defers to the Demoiselle's convener-direction without surfacing the lateral acquaintance, addresses substantive contributions to the senior PATRIARCHE rather than to the Demoiselle, and reads the Demoiselle's convener-frame as institutional architecture rather than as lateral peer-coordination. The senior PATRIARCHE reads the Demoiselle's composed convener-bearing and the Cavalier's reciprocal junior-attendee bearing as twin formations operating in calibrated parallel within the delegated institutional frame.

*The discipline is the joint operation of the Demoiselle's convener-frame as delegated institutional authority rather than as Demoiselle-substantive claim — the composed convener-bearing signals organisational competence without overstepping the senior partner's substantive authority over the matter; the Cavalier's reciprocal bearing signals reading of the institutional frame rather than of lateral peer-acquaintance. The senior PATRIARCHE reads the calibrated bearing as the marker of formed lateral peer-discipline that has internalised the institutional-frame distinction between convener-authority and substantive-claim.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same calibrated convener-bearing with the Demoiselle offering a brief composed substantive contribution within her own substantive area when the senior PATRIARCHE has explicitly invited her view — appropriate when the senior frame has explicitly opened the substantive moment within the convener's organisational function.

*The contemporary refinement when senior invitation has explicitly opened the substantive frame for the Demoiselle within her own area; the brief contribution operates within composed substantive register, never elaborated into convener-substituting Demoiselle-claim.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Surface the convener-authority through Demoiselle-display register that converts delegated organisational competence into substantive-rank claim; pre-empt the senior PATRIARCHE's substantive opening through convener-substantive contribution; address the Cavalier directly through convener-direction that signals lateral peer-coordination rather than institutional architecture; surface lateral peer-warmth toward the Cavalier across the Demoiselle's convener-functions; or under-claim the convener-authority through visible diffidence that converts delegated organisational standing into junior-shrink-from-frame.

*All five fail. The Demoiselle-display is "Convener-Display Authority" — the conversion of delegated organisational competence into substantive-rank claim the senior PATRIARCHE reads precisely as compositional gap. The substantive pre-emption is "Substantive-Lift Convener" — the breach of the senior PATRIARCHE's authority over the substantive opening through convener-substantive overreach. The Cavalier-direction is "Cavalier-Direction Push" — the conversion of institutional architecture into lateral peer-coordination the senior PATRIARCHE reads as compositional gap. The lateral warmth is "Senior-Frame Invocation" — the surfacing of personal-register that converts the institutional frame into lateral peer-acquaintance overlay. The convener under-claiming is "Junior-Convener Diffidence" — the visible diffidence that converts delegated organisational standing into junior-shrink-from-frame inappropriate to the convener-function.*

**Historical Context:** Le Déjeuner Professionnel for the Demoiselle-convened working-lunch is preserved at the Brussels gastronomic-establishment senior-firm tradition at Sea Grill, La Villa Lorraine, and Comme Chez Soi, where the delegated convener-authority architecture has been continuous practice across post-war generations of Belgian elite formation. The discipline operates equivalently in the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp senior-firm circles: at the Antwerp Diamond District commercial-elite working lunches the convener-bearing operates with marginally more direct register, while at the Ghent Korenlei patriciaat working lunches the calibration runs slower with additional cultural-substantive register.
