### Q9: La Discipline de Dégustation (The Host's Wine-Architecture Curation)

**Scenario:** At the host's own foundation cellar-tasting at the host's country residence near Spa — the host has curated a six-bottle vertical of a single Burgundian domaine spanning two decades, six guests are seated around the tasting table including two senior Patriarches with established wine-formation, one peer-Châtelaine, and two peer-Commandeurs. The architectural responsibility for the wine-curation rests with the host: the bottle-selection, the pour-sequence, the substantive frame, and the architectural close. The next thirty minutes calibrate whether the host has internalised the architectural Discipline de Dégustation — the curated wine-architecture that distinguishes the L3 architect-host from the L2 practitioner-taster.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Operate the curated wine-architecture as composed architect: open the substantive frame through brief composed reference to the vertical's architectural intent (the two-decade arc, the domaine's stylistic evolution, the cross-vintage substantive thread the curation invites), pour the first bottle in the calibrated sequence and offer brief composed substantive observation that opens space for the senior Patriarche cohort's substantive engagement rather than asserting architectural standing, calibrate the pour-rhythm to the senior Patriarche cohort's tasting-pace, sustain the architectural responsibility for the vertical's substantive arc across the six bottles without competing for substantive standing within any single bottle's discussion, and signal the architectural close at the appropriate sixth-bottle moment. The senior Patriarche cohort reads the calibrated host wine-curation as the Status Transfer signal of mature L3 host-formation — the discipline through which the host architects the wine-frame without performing the architect-role.

*The discipline is the architectural Discipline de Dégustation at host-curated register — the host operates the curated wine-architecture through composed architect-bearing that opens substantive space for the senior cohort rather than asserting architectural standing through wine-pulpit. The discipline carries the fivefold L3 architectural weight: the substantive-frame opening (avoiding architectural-standing claim), the calibrated pour-sequence (avoiding host-pace imposition), the substantive observation at architectural-opening register (avoiding wine-pulpit), the sustained vertical-arc responsibility (avoiding within-bottle substantive competition), and the architectural close signalling at the appropriate sixth-bottle moment (avoiding close-displacement). The senior cohort reads the calibrated host wine-curation as the merit signal of mature L3 architect-host formation.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same architectural wine-curation with a single composed substantive contribution within the host's own substantive area when the senior Patriarche cohort has explicitly opened the substantive thread to the host's area — appropriate when the architectural responsibility includes brief substantive contribution that advances the vertical's substantive arc rather than displacing it.

*The contemporary refinement when architectural responsibility includes brief substantive contribution; the contribution is composed and brief, anchored in the host's substantive area rather than in wine-pulpit display.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Open the substantive frame through wine-pulpit register that performs the architect-role through visible substantive claim; impose the host's pour-rhythm through faster pace than the senior Patriarche cohort's tasting-pace; surface the architectural standing through within-bottle substantive competition; signal the architectural close prematurely through host-anchored close-rhythm; develop host-narrative substantive thread across the vertical that the cluster registers as host-curation performance; or fail to read the vertical's substantive arc through visible bottle-by-bottle architectural fragmentation.

*All six fail. The wine-pulpit opening is "Curation-Pulpit Surface" — the conversion of architectural-frame opening into wine-pulpit display the senior Patriarche reads precisely as compositional gap. The pour-rhythm imposition is "Pour-Pace Impose" — the breach of senior tasting-pace through host-acceleration. The within-bottle competition is "Curation-Within-Bottle" — the host substantive standing claim within single-bottle discussion. The premature close is "Curation-Close Premature" — the breach of vertical-arc through host-anchored close. The host-narrative thread is "Curation-Narrative Surface" — the visible host-curation performance across the vertical. The bottle-by-bottle fragmentation is "Curation-Fragmentation" — the failure of vertical-arc reading.*

**Historical Context:** La Discipline de Dégustation at the architectural host-curated register is preserved at the Walloon foundation-cellar host-tradition at Spa, Stavelot, and Bouillon, and at the senior household-cellar host-evenings of Brabant Wallon. The convention runs across the francophone and Flemish elite-tasting senior host traditions in calibrated form: at the Antwerp commercial-elite senior host-tastings the architectural curation operates with marginally more direct register, while at the older Brussels gastronomic-establishment senior host-tastings at La Villa Lorraine and Bon-Bon the register carries the same composed architectural restraint across decades of preserved practice.

### Q10: Le Départ Mesuré (The Host's Architectural Close)

**Scenario:** At the conclusion of the four-hour foundation evening at the host's residence, the architectural close rests with the host. Several guests have begun to rise; the senior Patriarche cohort is calibrating their departure-rhythm; the host's architectural responsibility is to sustain the close-rhythm without imposing host-Tempo on the cohort's natural close, to manage the entrance-hall coat-collection architecture, to close each guest at composed warm farewell-register, and to manage the architectural close that shapes future invitations. The next thirty minutes calibrate whether the host has internalised the architectural Départ Mesuré — the host's architectural close that distinguishes the L3 architect from the L2 practitioner who has not yet hosted across the full architectural close.

**A) ✅ Good**

> Operate the architectural close at composed host-register: stand at the salon doorway as the senior Patriarche cohort signals their departure-rhythm, receive each departing guest at composed warm farewell-register that anchors their participation in the evening through brief substantive farewell-remark naming a specific moment of the evening, calibrate the farewell-register to each guest's standing (the senior Patriarche's farewell at marginally fuller substantive register than the peer-Châtelaine's, the peer-Châtelaine's at marginally fuller register than the established Commandeur's, the Cavalier's and Demoiselle's at the briefer composed warm register), absorb the entrance-hall coat-collection architecture through brief composed presence at the entrance, and close the architectural responsibility at the final guest's threshold-crossing. The host's architectural close shapes future invitations through the calibrated farewell-register: the senior Patriarche cohort reads the composed host-bearing as the Status Transfer signal that warrants future inclusion in the cohort's foundation-evenings; the peer-Châtelaine cohort reads the composed host-bearing as the architectural confirmation of mutual host-formation; the established Commandeur cohort reads the composed host-bearing as the architectural recognition that the host has internalised L3 formation; and the younger guest cohort reads the composed host-bearing as the Status Transfer signal that shapes their own formation toward L3 architect-host register over decades.

*The discipline is the architectural Départ Mesuré at host-close register — the host operates the architectural close through composed bearing that sustains the cohort's natural close-rhythm without imposing host-Tempo, calibrates farewell-register to each guest's standing, absorbs the entrance-hall coat-collection architecture, and closes the architectural responsibility at the final guest's threshold-crossing. The discipline carries the sevenfold L3 architectural weight: the salon-doorway position (avoiding architectural absence), the composed warm farewell-register (avoiding effusion or coldness), the substantive farewell-remark (anchoring participation), the calibrated standing-register differential (avoiding flat farewell-register), the entrance-hall absorption (avoiding architectural neglect of coat-collection), the final-guest closing (avoiding premature architectural close), and the Status Transfer signal across all guest-cohorts (avoiding architectural blindness to the formation-shaping function). The senior cohort reads the calibrated architectural close as the merit signal of mature L3 architect-host formation, and the architectural close itself shapes future invitations across the foundation-cohort calendar.*

**B) 🟡 Slightly different**

> The same architectural close with a brief private exchange at the threshold with one departing guest when the substantive overlap from the evening warrants the brief continuation — appropriate when the substantive thread has explicitly opened the brief threshold-moment within the broader architectural close.

*The contemporary refinement when substantive thread warrants brief threshold-moment; the moment is composed and bounded, never elaborated into private extended departure that displaces the architectural close architecture for the broader cohort.*

**C) ❌ Would not do that**

> Impose host-Tempo on the cohort's natural close-rhythm through visible host-anchoring; surface the architectural close through performative host-bearing that the senior Patriarche cohort registers as compositional gap; flatten the farewell-register across all guest-standings through undifferentiated composed warmth; abandon the salon-doorway position through extended cluster-engagement during the close; develop host-narrative across the architectural close through visible substantive farewell-narrative; close the architectural responsibility prematurely through visible host-fatigue at the entrance-hall; or fail to read the Status Transfer signal function of the architectural close through visible architectural-close as practical-end rather than as formation-shaping moment.

*All seven fail. The host-Tempo imposition is "Close-Tempo Impose" — the breach of cohort natural close-rhythm through host-anchoring that the senior Patriarche cohort reads precisely as compositional gap. The performative host-bearing is "Performative Host-Close" — the visible performance of the architect-close. The flattened farewell-register is "Farewell-Register Flat" — the undifferentiated composed warmth that the standing-differential cohort reads as architectural compositional gap. The salon-doorway abandonment is "Close-Position Abandon" — the architectural absence at the close-position. The host-narrative is "Close-Narrative Surface" — the visible substantive farewell-narrative. The premature architectural close is "Close-Premature Architectural" — the visible host-fatigue at the entrance-hall. The Status-Transfer blindness is "Close-Transfer Blindness" — the failure to read the architectural close's formation-shaping function across guest-cohorts.*

**Historical Context:** Le Départ Mesuré at the architectural host-close register is preserved at the older Brussels patrician townhouse architectural-close tradition of Uccle, Watermael, Boitsfort, Tervuren, and Stockel, where the host architectural-close discipline has been continuously calibrated across post-war generations of Belgian elite host-formation. The convention persists in calibrated form across the francophone Brussels and Flemish Antwerp host-traditions: at the Antwerp commercial-elite host-evenings the architectural close carries marginally more direct register in keeping with Antwerp commercial confidence, while at the Liège Cercle senior bourgeois host-evenings the architectural close runs marginally warmer in keeping with the Walloon convivial register without surrendering the calibrated host-architecture-close discipline.
